All Entertainment Venues in Changsha Are Closed

The Municipal Office Forcibly Collects Entertainment Tax

The Entire Drama Industry Holds a Large-Scale Petition

Changsha Correspondence: There are 11 movie theaters in Changsha City, including Far East, Pingping, Baihe, YMCA, etc. There is one Peking opera theater, Dihua; five Cantonese opera theaters: Xiangchun, Jingxing, Jixiang, Xinwutai, Far East; and only one modern drama theater, Changsha. The highest ticket price is only 30 cents, and the lowest is only 16 copper coins. Business is not very developed. Guo Fangrui, the head of the Changsha Municipal Preparatory Office, studied in France under the work-study program and has only been in office for two months. His first policy was to petition the provincial government to collect a 10% entertainment tax to subsidize the education expenses of elementary schools in Changsha City. The 174th regular meeting of the provincial government resolved to approve the collection, but the tax rate was reduced to 5%. Director Guo then notified all entertainment venues that it would be implemented from June 1st, tasking each theater with collecting and remitting the tax when selling tickets. The theaters agreed to support the tax collection since the funds were to be taken from the audience, and the theaters would not suffer any losses. However, they felt that the tax collection was too meticulous, involving the rounding of fractions and zeroing of totals, and the procedures were cumbersome. They requested that the government directly send personnel to collect the tax from the audience at each theater instead of them acting as the agents. Director Guo did not agree and ordered each theater to deduct 5 yuan of entertainment tax for every 100 yuan of business income each day. The theaters believed that this method, ostensibly collected from the audience, was actually deducted from the theater owners. The theaters had already paid business tax, police licensing fees, stamp tax, etc., which amounted to a large sum. Adding another burden was beyond their ability. Therefore, they unanimously opposed it and requested that the government still directly collect the tax. If they were required to be responsible for collecting the tax, they requested a reduction in the tax rate. After several exchanges of official documents and negotiations, the final result was that Director Guo still insisted on his collection proposal, but allowed old-style operas to actually pay 3%, with 2% as a collection fee, and movies to actually pay 4%, with 1% as a collection fee.

The theater owners felt that the amount of tax was too fractional and could not be collected from the audience. Since the theater owners were to bear the burden, they requested that it be changed to a package deal, with each theater paying a certain amount of entertainment tax per month based on its business size, in order to save all the trouble. Unexpectedly, Director Guo not only insisted on not agreeing but also sent troops to close all entertainment venues in Changsha City at 6:00 PM on the 25th, posting a notice at the entrance of each theater stating, "Notice: According to the order of the Hunan Provincial Department of Construction, the case of collecting entertainment tax to subsidize the education expenses of elementary schools in the urban area has been resolved by the 174th regular meeting of the Provincial Government Committee, and it has been approved to collect 5% of the ticket price of entertainment venues. It has been approved to start collecting on June 1st and a notice has been issued ordering the theater to comply. However, each tax collector reported that the theater made excuses and refused to collect the tax. The above situation was reported to the Department of Construction for instructions, and an order was received to strictly enforce it. Yesterday, a recorded order was forwarded. Despite repeated orders, the theater still deliberately held back and made excuses, which is extremely contemptuous. It should be immediately sealed off together with the military police and await verification."

That night, the Changsha City Drama Industry Association held an emergency meeting, attended by more than 1,000 male and female members. The following resolutions were made: (1) At 12:00 AM on the 26th, all members would gather and petition the Party and government agencies, explaining that the people only have the obligation to pay taxes and not the right to collect taxes for the government. They would still request the government to directly collect the entertainment tax, quickly lift the closure, and restore business in order to maintain the livelihoods of thousands of people. (2) Issue a declaration asking all sectors to uphold justice. (3) Schedule a meeting with the press to report on the progress of the situation and ask for assistance. It is still unknown how this matter will be resolved. (June 26)

Resolution of the Litigation Case Between Jinan Telephone Company and Japanese Merchant

Telephone Company Wins, East Development Loses

Jinan Correspondence: In the case of the litigation between the Jinan Telephone Company and the Japanese merchant East Development Co., Ltd. over debt, the Jinan District Court of First Instance made a two-tiered judgment: (1) ordered the Telephone Company to compensate East Development 420,000 Japanese yen; (2) granted a provisional attachment of the Telephone Company's assets. The Telephone Company was dissatisfied and appealed to the Shandong Higher Court in two tiers. The Higher Court believed that this case concerned the transportation sovereignty of the entire Jinan City internally and extraterritoriality externally. A slight error in the trial would have a significant impact. Therefore, it was extremely cautious. After half a year, the judgment was made a few days ago, also in two tiers: (1) East Development's request for a provisional disposition of the Telephone Company's assets was rejected; (2) East Development's request for the Telephone Company to repay 420,000 Japanese yen was also rejected. East Development lost the case, and the Telephone Company won. The case was completely resolved. The main text of the Higher Court's judgment is recorded as follows: The original judgment regarding the defendant, Jinan Telephone Company, being jointly and severally liable to compensate the plaintiff, Japanese yen, principal and interest, totaling 420,000 yen, and bearing the costs of litigation, is hereby changed. The appellant's claim in the first instance regarding the foregoing is dismissed. The appellant's application for provisional execution is dismissed. The costs of the second instance litigation shall be borne by the appellant.

Han Bandit Peng Ruiting Arrested for Impersonating a Military Commander

Xuzhou Correspondence: Peng Ruiting, a bandit from the junction of northern Xuzhou and southern Shandong, has been causing trouble in the Hanzhuang area. Chen Shaohan's department of the 42nd Regiment of the 7th Division, stationed in Hanzhuang, had conducted strict investigations but failed to capture him. Unexpectedly, after the bandit suppression in southern Shandong, Peng Bandit could not hide his tracks in Han, so he had a whim and came to Xuzhou posing as a brigade commander of the guard army, using the alias Peng Guangzhu, and staying at the Fulai Inn on Er Malu in the eastern railway station. Chen Xueshun, the director of the Xuzhou Military and Police Supervision Office, initially received a report from Chen Chuanjing, the second battalion commander of the 42nd Regiment, requesting his arrest, and then received a report from the machine gun company of the 42nd Regiment that a false military officer, Peng Guangzhu, was hiding in Xuzhou. He also received a report from the Fulai Inn that a fake military officer was staying there. Therefore, on the evening of the 25th, he sent a team to arrest him. Peng Ruiting was captured on the spot, and a private seal, three passports, one travel permit, three lieutenant colonel symbols, and three lieutenant symbols were confiscated. He was escorted to the office. After interrogation, it was confirmed that Peng Guangzhu was indeed the alias of the Han bandit Peng Ruiting. The evidence has been collected, and the bandit has been sent to the garrison headquarters for interrogation. (28th)

Cai Guo Jingluan Has Taken the Remains of the May 3rd Martyrs to the Capital

Oppose the Temporary Burial of the Remains of the May 3rd Martyrs

Jinan Quick Dispatch on the 27th: The excavation of the backyard of the former Japanese Concession in Jinan, which uncovered the remains and clothing of the martyrs who died in the May 3rd Incident after being cremated by the Japanese, has attracted great attention at home and abroad. The Preparatory Committee for the Commemoration of the Martyrs of the May 3rd Incident resolved at its sixth meeting on the 26th to place the remains of the martyrs in magnetic jars for temporary burial. An engineer was also assigned to survey the site of the martyrs' tomb, and Zhang Honglie, the director of the Department of Construction, was tasked with designing the construction. However, Guo Jingluan, the wife of Cai Gongshi, did not agree with this method. Therefore, at 10:35 AM today (the 27th), she took the 201st Pingpu train from Jinan back to Shanghai, packing the remains of the martyrs into a large leather suitcase and carrying it with her. The suitcase had already been tagged, but Mrs. Cai was afraid of losing it, so she took it back and kept it by her side. By the time the local authorities in Shandong learned of this, the train had already departed and could not be stopped.

In front of the building of the Concession, the people listed from right to left were: (1) Li Jiangqiu, a journalist stationed in Jinan; (2) Mrs. Guo Jingluan; (3) Xin Changsheng, a worker at the Concession who escaped at the same time as the late martyr Cai Gongshi; and the rest were excavators. The one standing tall was the excavator. The jar contained the remains and clothing of the martyrs excavated.

The Truth About the Rice Shuangzhen Case in Liaoning

Shenyang Correspondence: The Japanese police in the Japanese-affiliated land in Liaoning County灌死回民米雙珍Case, after Liaoyang County negotiated with the Japanese side and提出懲兇賠償The Japanese side has always been reluctant to admit their fault, which has aroused public outrage in Liaoyang and organized a support association. Muslims are even more indignant. The Qingzhen Church has held several meetings to discuss response measures and urge the county authorities to negotiate seriously. All sectors in Shenyang have also been speaking out in support of this case. In order to be cautious, the Liaoyang District Court Prosecutor's Office especially took 100 grams of liquid from the lungs of Rice's body when Dr. Wei Chenguang (English) of the Liaoyang Official Hospital dissected Rice's corpse, put it in a bottle and sealed it, and sent it to the Liaoning Higher Court Prosecutor's Office a few days ago, which transferred it to the Xiaoheyan Shi Hospital for detailed chemical tests. After the doctor's chemical test, it proved that it was indeed a mixture of cold water and kerosene, and there were no tuberculosis bacteria in it. The doctor issued an appraisal report and returned the original test object to the High Inspection Office, which reported the situation to the provincial government and asked it to transfer it to the Diplomatic Commissioner's Office to negotiate seriously with the Japanese side. The Liaoning National Diplomacy Association believed that the case was related to people's lives and sent Zhu Huanjie, a cadre of the association, to Liaoyang to conduct an on-site investigation to clarify the truth. Zhu returned on the 24th and told reporters that Rice Shuangzhen had been running a beef shop in the Liaoyang affiliated land, with a small capital and was self-sufficient. He was also very upright in his daily life. Because a Japanese woman, Ms. Onishi, lived in the same courtyard, who made a living by lending money at high interest rates, and had been out collecting debts for several days, the Japanese police suspected that Rice had harmed her and sent her to the police station to force a confession. Rice naturally could not admit it because he really did not know anything about it. The Japanese police then used vicious means to pour kerosene into Rice's mouth and nose, injuring his lungs and killing him. The Japanese police, because there was no real confession, caused a human life and falsely claimed that Rice died of lung disease and ordered his family to take the corpse back. Rice's family then reported to the Chinese official. After the county government sent personnel to the scene to examine the corpse, they could not prove the cause of death, so they ordered his family to hold a burial ceremony according to Islamic rites. They then sent the corpse to the hospital for dissection and saw that one lobe of the deceased's lung was swollen and one lobe was shrunken. Although an examination was carried out at the time, it was not possible to determine the cause of death. Now it has been completely proven, and the case is clear. The Japanese side should be fully responsible for Rice's death. It is also heard that Ms. Onishi returned once a few days after Rice's death, and then disappeared. It is thought that the Japanese side had ordered her to hide or send her far away for fear of causing our side's accusation. (June 24)

The Murderer of Xuehua Commits Suicide in Harbin

Fan Xusui Throws Himself into the River and Commits Suicide

Seven Pawn Tickets Were Found Beside Him

Harbin Communication on the 24th: The case of the brutal murder of the prostitute Xuehua in the Daiwa Hotel has been under strict investigation by police detectives day and night. It is generally believed that Fan has no sufficient travel funds and no sufficient time. He is still hiding in this port. Therefore, the search for him at his relatives and friends is very strict. On the 24th of this month, the Songhua River Water Rescue Team discovered a male corpse in the river and pulled it to the shore. After police verification, it was the fugitive criminal Fan Xusui who had been arrested. He had committed suicide in fear of crime. The discovery of the corpse was due to the fact that the iron pipe of the river channel in the Daoli Toutou Street Tongjiangbin Waterway, which discharges sewage, was suddenly blocked. Workers from the Naval River Transportation Office were working early in the morning and heard a sound and suspected something. Several people went to investigate and suddenly saw that the end of the iron pipe draining water was blocked by a corpse. They reported it to the Special City Water Rescue Team, which rescued it and dragged it to the shore. Afterwards, Tian Xiuzhi, a patrol officer from the Jiangqiao East Police Station, came to investigate and saw that his appearance was similar to the fugitive criminal Fan Xusui who was wanted by the Second Office. He then told the Second Office, which verified that it was correct and transferred it to the Municipal First Hospital in the afternoon and placed it in the mortuary with the victim Xuehua. After the examination, it will be buried. Fan was wearing a blue silk long gown, green western-style trousers, and yellow leather shoes when he died. There were 20 yuan of banknotes, a watch, and seven pawn tickets in his pocket. The dates of his pledges were not very long. His body was not damaged by water. Therefore, it is generally speculated that Fan killed Xuehua because he had no hope for the future and because he had spent too much money and could not continue. He was angry and killed Xuehua. After Xuehua's death, he could not escape, so he threw himself into the river on the evening of the 22nd, so the corpse was not rotten. As for the deceased Xuehua, her parents and a younger brother and sister are still alive. Their daily support depended on Xuehua. Now that she has been killed, her parents are crying in grief and almost do not want to live.

The Province is Divided into Eight Major Districts

Coal and Electricity Material Prices are High; Jointly Petition for Relief

If they are suddenly ordered to stop, it will affect education, which is no small matter. They should separately raise funds to maintain education. However, the situations in each county are different, and the methods of compensation are difficult to standardize. It was resolved to order each county to immediately convene the Finance and Education Bureaus to properly devise compensation methods and submit them for review and transfer. Those that have not yet implemented sutra recitation donations will not be allowed to implement them again. Yesterday, the county government received the provincial order to comply and was required to report the annual donation amount of Wuxi's sutra recitation donations for record.

Record of Interrogation of Private Production of Inferior Silkworm Eggs: Wei Zhizhong, the former director of the Tian Shang Shi Qian Administrative Bureau, was found to be privately producing inferior silkworm eggs. Li Songwen, a local villager, wrote to the Sericulture Suppression Office to investigate, and it was confirmed to be true. Wei Heyuan, who produced the eggs, as well as many inferior eggs, were handed over by the Thirteenth Branch of the Public Security Bureau to the county government for interrogation. Yesterday, County Magistrate Pan sent police to escort Wei Zhizhong, Wei Heyuan, and Wei Peiqi, along with the evidence, to the county. The court immediately opened to question them. Wei Zhizhong claimed that he did not privately produce inferior eggs. Last year, he gathered shares to organize the Sanyou Egg Production Farm, which was solely operated by Wei Heyuan. He did not inquire about the private production matters. Wei Peiqi's statement was similar. Wei Heyuan said that the egg production farm was rented from Zhizhong and Peiyuan. After the sale was poor, it was closed down. The silkworm eggs searched this time were used for his own breeding. The lead ring was also left over from last year. County Magistrate Pan, based on the confession, said that Wei Heyuan admitted to privately producing eggs in the Public Security Bureau, so how could he deny it? He immediately ordered him to be sent to prison. Wei Zhizhong and Wei Peiqi were temporarily released on bail by the shopkeeper, pending investigation and handling.

Recent Situation of the Rice Market: The rice market in Xidi gradually rose one month ago, with a great upward trend. However, recently the weather has turned clear, and the sources from various places are also strong. The price of rice has fallen as a result. The current market price of rough japonica rice is 3.5 yuan per shi, and white japonica rice is 10.08 yuan, which is two yuan less than the peak price. According to a recent survey of rice storage, there are 500,000 shi of japonica rice, 300,000 shi of indica rice, and more than 100,000 shi of rough indica, white indica, and rough japonica rice. Although the amount of storage is not very large, there is no way out. All rice merchants are worried.

Four-Year-Old Child Drowns in a Pit: Xie Xingkui from Jiangyin and his wife, Wang, live at No. 3 Housheng Lane, Chen Baitou Lane, Tonghui Road. Xingkui is currently a clerk at Wanxiang Trough. He has a son named Xingda, who is four years old. Three days ago, the child suddenly disappeared. He was searched for everywhere but could not be found. Yesterday morning around 7:00, the child was suddenly found in the pit toilet of the Tianzhang Tea Shop near Tonghui Bridge. Someone reported it to his mother, Xie Wang, who went to identify it. It was indeed Xingda's body. People were immediately ordered to fish it out and support the body for a painful cry, which was heartbreaking.

Changzhou

Reorganization of the Shipping Association: The Wuyi Shipping Association was ordered to reorganize. On the 28th, executive and supervisory committee members were elected at the Xinqiao Elementary School in Ximen. Party and government agencies sent personnel to monitor. As a result of the election, Wu Kang, Fan Baizhu, Fu Zhongyi, Liu Peisheng, Wu Jincheng, Yang Chengkan, Shi Zemin, and others were elected as executive committee members. Ma Qiji, Wu Junmin, Jiang Shihua, Sheng Zhaoji, Zhuang Zhijun, and others were elected as supervisory committee members. Wu Kang was elected as the chairman of the executive committee.

Woman Commits Suicide by Drowning: A ship sailing from Zhouqiao Town in Wuyi to Wuxi was passing through the Hutangqiao area in the Sixth District at around 2:00 PM on the 28th. Suddenly, a middle-aged woman on the ship jumped out of the cabin for unknown reasons and committed suicide by jumping into the river. Passengers on the ship were panicked, so they stopped the ship and tried to salvage the body, but it took a long time.

Changshu

Maidservant with the Surname Xi Commits Suicide by Poison: Xi Yunzhong, residing at No. 27 Tonghe Bridge Alley, Datian'an, outside the South Gate of this county, employed a maidservant named Tao Damei from Hupu. Tao is currently 22 years old and quite beautiful. Damei was originally at Miss Xi's for three years. Later, she became acquainted with Lao San, the second son of Yunzhong. Later, Yunzhong ordered Damei to pretend to smoke opium and had a relationship with Damei. Gao, the wife of Lao San, heard about this, but she could not do anything because she was favored by her mother-in-law. As a result, Damei became more powerful. On the 27th of this month, due to a minor matter of cooking meat, Damei was scolded by Gao and told Yunzhong, but he did not help her. Damei was very angry and quietly swallowed opium to commit suicide. At that time, the Xi family thought that this was the result of Gao's scolding, and everyone made things difficult for her. The matter was leaked out, and neighbors came to watch. However, the Xi family was afraid that the matter would escalate and immediately closed the gate to reject visitors. On the one hand, they wanted to lock Gao's feet to the corpse. Fortunately, Gao escaped through the side door. Knowing that the matter could not be concealed, the Xi family reported to the family of the maidservant and came to the city to discuss. They falsely claimed that she died suddenly from Sha fever. On the other hand, they also reported to the place and requested an examination. They waited for the family of the corpse to come to the city to discuss using money and a generous burial for the deceased as conditions. The family of the corpse then requested the county to waive the examination, but Shen Cheng, the reviewer of the county government, was afraid of repeating the Ximen murder case and rejected it. On the one hand, he still telegraphed Dr. Xie Tang to accompany Shen Cheng, the reviewer, to the corpse site outside the South Gate at 9:00 PM for examination. As a result, Dr. Xie examined and found that the deceased had indeed died from smoking opium before her death. He ordered the Xi family to give a generous burial, and the coffin was taken back by the family.

The Provincial Security Team Captures a Major Bandit: The major bandit Wang Fengyi and others had committed numerous crimes before Ma Yuren's time, but Wang lived peacefully in Hupu, in this county, and no one dared to arrest him. This year, after the Pacification and Security Army came to garrison in this county, the battalion headquarters dispatched the Sixth Infantry Company to garrison in Hupu, and everything was peaceful. On the evening of the 27th, Company Commander Chen received a secret letter reporting that bandits were hiding in the house of a Pan family in this port. Company Commander Chen then gathered the local security and sent some soldiers to the upstairs of the Pan family. As expected, they captured Chen Changwan. They took him back to the company headquarters for detailed interrogation. Chen confessed that there were still Lu Rujin and the boss Wang Fengyi staying in this town. That night, Company Commander Chen captured Wang and Lu one after another. On the morning of the 28th, he personally escorted them to the battalion headquarters in the city. Battalion Commander Shen Yiming personally investigated them. Bandit Wang confessed and cunningly denied any banditry. Lu Rujin claimed that he was not a bandit and was currently a detective in the 13th Water Police Team. Later, due to the nature of his duties, he was inevitably implicated by the bandits. Battalion Commander Shen then used the telephone to ask the 13th Team if there was such a detective. Team Leader Yang Qingjiu proved that he was indeed a detective in his team. Patrol Officer Wang Jiarong was then dispatched to the camp headquarters in the North Gate to request bail. Battalion Commander Shen handed Lu Rujin over to Patrol Officer Wang to take away. Wang and Chen were temporarily detained in the Public Security Bureau detention center.

Nantong

Wang Boqun and His Wife Leave Nantong to Return to Beijing: Minister of Communications Wang Boqun, along with his wife, Ms. Bao Zhining, came to Nantong on the Emei Wheel on the 27th to wish Bao a happy birthday. They stayed on the ship that night. On the 28th, they toured the Five Parks in the south of the city. In the evening, local people from all walks of life held a public banquet at the club. Wang told reporters that this trip was entirely for personal matters. At present, the suppression of the communists in Jiangxi is in the final offensive stage, and there are many important matters in Beijing. He stayed on the ship and could handle important telegrams at any time. Wang and his wife took the original wheel back to Beijing on the 29th.

The Second Batch of Wounded Soldiers Learning Skills Arrives in Nantong: The 11th Division of the Army stationed in Hankou sent Zhuang Mingyuan to Nantong to establish a wounded soldiers' skill learning factory. The first batch of 84 people has been working for more than half a month. The second batch of 140 wounded soldiers arrived in Nantong on the De'an Wheel on the evening of the 27th.

Investigate the Road Construction Costs of Soldiers and Workers: The Nantong City Yao Road implemented soldiers and workers. The Construction Bureau reported expenses of more than 9,000 yuan. The 280th Regiment stated that the soldiers and workers' food expenses were all paid by the regiment headquarters. The police team also stated that there was no receipt or payment. The county government implemented an investigation.

Jiangyin

District Representative Assembly Elects Executive and Supervisory Committee Members: The First District Party Department Representative Assembly was originally scheduled to be held on the 25th, but because the County Rectification Committee had some points to explain, it telegraphed the province for instructions and changed the meeting to the 28th. Twenty representatives attended the meeting. The election supervisor was Wang Shusheng, and the chairman was Liu Youkang. The most important issue was the discussion of Huang Bingying and Zhang Shaoting's impeachment of Zhu Tianying, the head of the First District and the head of the County Rectification Committee, and Li Jialing, the head of the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau, for having major suspicions in the case of dividing opium. They should be suspended from their duties and sent to the Wu County District Court for investigation. The election began in the afternoon. As a result of the vote, Wang Bingchu, Han Qingbai, and Tang Kesheng were elected as executive committee members, Chen Dasan and Zhou Guotang were elected as alternate executive committee members, Wang Ying was elected as a supervisory committee member, and Qian Yaojiang was elected as an alternate supervisory committee member.

Zhenjiang

Director of the Wujin Construction Bureau Accused: Since the provincial government moved to Zhenjiang, cases of county magistrates and bureau directors coming to the province to file complaints have emerged one after another. Recently, in addition to Wang Ma, a woman from Tongshan County, coming to the province to file a complaint against Yang, the county magistrate, yesterday afternoon, representatives of people's organizations from Wujin County, Wang Qiyi, Gao Fuji, and He Gongbai, went to the Provincial Construction Department to petition that Sheng Ban, the director of the Wujin County Construction Bureau, had committed various illegal and harmful acts. They requested that he be dismissed and investigated and submitted a written statement listing his various crimes. After receiving the statement, the Construction Department ordered the Wujin County Magistrate to investigate and handle the matter.

Former Chairman of the Anti-Japanese Association Sentenced: Xue Zhenglin, the former chairman of the Zhenjiang Anti-Japanese Association, had many discrepancies in his accounts during his tenure, and his receipts were incomplete. After being investigated by the County Supervisory Committee, he was reported to the Jiangsu Provincial Party Department. The Provincial Party Department also believed that the difference between his income and expenditure was too large and suspected embezzlement. In addition to suspending his party membership, he was transferred to the court for trial. After repeated investigations and interrogations by the court, yesterday Xue Zhenglin and Dai Jizhi, the former accountant of the Anti-Japanese Association, were jointly sentenced to four months of imprisonment for the crime of continuous embezzlement.

Gaoyou

Kidnapping in Gaogui Township: More than a dozen bandits armed with guns suddenly came to Gaogui Township in the tenth district of the county the day before yesterday. They first searched the home of Wang Kuiwen. His son resisted the bandits and was shot. They then went to Wang Fuxi's home and searched extensively. Before leaving, they kidnapped his eight-year-old son. Full County Population Statistics: County Magistrate Wang was previously ordered to investigate the population and has instructed the district chiefs to comply. The districts have now completed their investigations and reported them. The total number of households in the county is 127,290, with 324,830 men and 302,948 women. There are 114,672 men and 6,248 women who can read.

Danyang

Robbery and Injury in Dengjiacun: Multiple bandits wielding sharp weapons broke into the home of Deng Xu in Dengjiacun, eastern township, last night, ransacking the place. They twisted Deng Xu and burned her. Her grandson heard the alarm and came to the rescue, but was wounded in the leg by the bandits. After an inventory, a total of more than 500 yuan in silver jewelry was lost. The case has been reported to the police for investigation.

Resisting Arrest and Assaulting Police in Chenjianong: The Fourth Public Security Bureau of Fangxian Bridge heard that gambling often took place in the teahouse opened by Chen Jifu in Chenjianong. They dispatched a patrol to investigate and arrest the gamblers. Four gamblers were arrested on the spot and taken to the bureau along with the gambling equipment. Unexpectedly, when they were about four li away from the village, a group of villagers snatched the gamblers and injured several patrol officers. When Bureau Chief Cao heard the news, he dispatched Patrol Officer Wang with more police to arrest them, but they were also beaten by the villagers. The case has been reported to the county bureau for handling.

Huzhou

The Case of Attempted Robbery of the Ding Family Has Been Cracked: The Qingxiang Bureau of Wuxing County, this city, ordered the detective team to crack the case of the attempted robbery of Ding Kuichen's home in Anxuedong on the 7th of this month. After receiving the order, Team Leader Wu supervised the detectives to seriously investigate the case. The investigation revealed that the case was related to Zhou Huanchen, a habitual thief. Yesterday, the detectives of the team met the thief in front of the Xinsheng Pawnshop on Nanjie in this city and immediately arrested him and took him to the team. Team Leader Hu ordered the detectives to go to Cuijianong in Dongmen and retrieve items such as tin candlesticks from the thief's mistress's place and take them to the team together. After being questioned by Team Leader Hu, Zhou Huanchen confessed that he was 45 years old, from Wuyu, and made weaving machines. He currently lived in Cuijianong. The incident that occurred at the Ding residence in Xuegongdouding on the night of the 7th of this month was initiated by Xu Longbao. There was another person from Anhui whose name was unknown. They used a bamboo ladder to climb in from the back door. I was waiting outside for him. Not long after, the two of them came out and said to me, "They know inside, and now they want to make a phone call. Let's go!" So the three of us separated and left. Whether there were knives or guns, I did not see. After receiving the confession, Team Leader Hu reported it to the Qingxiang Bureau of Wuxing County for handling.

Kidnapping in Lianhuadou: A resident named Shanshang Ashun in Lianhuadou, Shenglin Village, Sixth District of Wuxing County, has some assets and can make a decent living. However, on the night of the 26th, more than a dozen bandits armed with guns broke down the door and entered, searching and looting at will, taking away all the clothes and silver dollars. Before leaving, they kidnapped Ashun's son.

Bengbu

The Attached Land of the Barracks Has Been Surveyed: Hu Qin and others from the First Investigation Team sent by the Ministry of Military Affairs to Bengbu to survey and map detailed diagrams of the Bengbu Xiaoshan South Barracks and attached land for the purpose of reorganization have reported to the Ministry of Military Affairs. According to the report, the Bengbu barracks were purchased by the former Anhui Governor Ni Sichong during the seventh year of the Republic of China (1918) to build the Yangtze River Inspection Envoy's Office and barracks. In addition to some barracks that have already been built, the Public Security Bureau of this port sent personnel together with personnel from Fengyang County to demarcate the boundaries of the barracks and set up boundary stakes. The survey and measurement have now been completed. The management and other matters should be taken over by the military. After receiving the report, the Ministry of Military Affairs stated that the land attached to the Bengbu barracks had been paid for military use. It should be managed by the ministry in accordance with the regulations for the management of military property. The survey and measurement have now been completed, and boundary stakes have been set up. Personnel have been dispatched to reorganize the site. The Anhui Provincial Government was ordered to instruct the Bengbu Public Security Bureau to comply with the order and assist properly, and to instruct its subordinates to be informed. After receiving the order, the Public Security Bureau has complied with the order.

Nanjing, 29th - The Ministry of Education issued a circular to various consulates abroad regarding the deadline for registration of overseas Chinese schools, extending it by another year from July 1st.

Executive Committee Meeting of the China Vocational Guidance Organization Federation

Passed Nine Important Resolutions

Grand Meeting to be Held in Zhenjiang on August 2nd

Discussing Practical and Concrete Measures

The Executive Committee of the National Federation of Vocational Guidance Organizations of China held its second session at the Jiading Vocational Guidance Center the day before yesterday (the 28th) at 9:00 AM. The details of the meeting are recorded below:

Attending Representatives: From vocational guidance centers: Pan Yangyao, Gan Chunquan, Zhao Wenlong, Wu Zongwen from Shanghai, Lu Linxun from Jiading, Wu Xixia from Wu County, 芮子玉 Rui Ziyu from Wuxi, Xie Yicheng from Nanjing. From education bureaus: Yang Zhuofu from Jiading, Liu Jian from Zhenjiang (replaced by Yang Zhuofu). Others: Jiang Wenyu and Zhou Kaisen from the China Vocational Education Society, Gao Jiansi from the Jiangsu Provincial Educational College, Zhang Zhonghuan from the Provincial Shanghai Middle School, He Qingru from the Young Men's Christian Association (replaced by Pan Yangyao), Feng Baoling from the Chinese Engineering Society, Chen Qingshi from Great China University, Liu Zhanen from Soochow University.

Passed Resolutions: 1. The proposal for this federation to apply for registration for the record. (Resolved) The China Vocational Education Society will revise the draft application and take the lead in applying for registration for the record. 2. The proposal for the second annual meeting and the National Vocational Education Organization Discussion Meeting organized by the China Vocational Education Society to be held at the same time. (Resolved) (1) To be held at the same time as the China Vocational Education Discussion Meeting in Zhenjiang Boxian Park at 9:00 AM on August 2nd. Each member will be notified separately immediately, and representatives will be recommended, and the number of people will be reported to send train tickets. (2) To attend the National Vocational Education Discussion Meeting on August 1st, the Vocational Guidance Discussion Conference on the morning of August 2nd, and the report and review meeting in the afternoon. (3) Each organization will recommend one to three representatives to attend. (4) This session's proposal should focus on the difficulties encountered in practice and the problems that urgently need to be resolved, and concrete measures should be proposed. 3. The proposal for this federation to ask the National Government to issue a general order to the education departments of various provinces to quickly establish rural vocational normal education organizations to cultivate teachers and benefit guidance. (Resolved) Jiang Wenyu was elected to review and revise it before submitting it to the government for a general order to the education departments of various provinces to implement it. 4. The proposal to request the central government to stipulate that public funds should be used to handle the relief work for beggars and vagrants. (Resolved) To expand the original proposal and add the management of industrial production centers, public canteens, and public lodging houses, Jiang Wenyu and Guangsheng were still elected to review and revise it, and the central government was requested to issue a general order to the provinces, cities, and counties to implement it. 5. The proposal to expand vocational education guidance research and publicity. (Resolved) To jointly organize a committee of vocational guidance experts, member organizations, and vocational guidance workers in schools at all levels to take on the responsibilities of writing and editing, and Jiang Wenyu, Yang Weiyu, and Pan Yangyao were elected to contact major newspapers in Beijing and Shanghai about a vocational guidance column every half month to report on this area's essays and events. 6. The date and location of the third Executive Committee meeting. (Resolved) To be determined after the Zhenjiang discussion meeting. 7. The naming of this federation's second annual meeting. (Resolved) To be named the National Vocational Guidance Discussion Conference. 8. The proposal for this federation's Zhenjiang Vocational Guidance Discussion Meeting to recommend preparatory committee members. (Resolved) The Zhenjiang County Education Bureau, Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce, and Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center were recommended as preparatory committee members. 9. Gu Qiaoruo was elected to go to Jiangsu and Zhejiang to investigate and entrusted him to investigate the vocational guidance and student exits in various counties.

Representative Speeches: During this Executive Committee meeting, each representative attended the meeting at the Jiading Vocational Guidance Center. They were invited by the local Education Bureau and 20 other groups from the party headquarters and other organizations to give speeches at the Jiading County Junior High School and the Jiading Public Education Museum. The speakers included Jiang Wenyu, Chen Qingshi, Zhang Zhonghuan, Pan Yangyao, etc. There were no fewer than 500 listeners. The topics were generally about guidance on further education and employment. The weather was very hot that day, but the listeners were all delighted. After the speeches, the local art experts were publicly invited by various groups to dress up and perform noble entertainment to welcome each executive committee member. The meeting ended at around 5:00 PM.

McTyeire School

Shanghai McTyeire School held its graduation ceremony yesterday (the 29th) at 4:00 PM at the school. This year's graduating class includes 21 students from the high school department, 32 from junior high, and 53 from the sixth grade of elementary school. The ceremony was held as usual. Weihaiwei Road Minzhi Middle School and its affiliated elementary school and kindergarten held a joint graduation ceremony yesterday. Principal Xu Renhan presided over the ceremony. Over five hundred guests, family members, teachers, and students attended. Japanese Players Win in Mixed Doubles

Oda's Triple Jump and Nanbu's Long Jump

Both Set New Japanese Records

(Dentsu Tokyo, 29th) In preparation for the Far Eastern Games, track and field events were held yesterday at Koshien Stadium. Oda Mikio, Japan's leading figure in jumping events, achieved a distance of 15.48 meters in the triple jump, setting a new Japanese record. He also achieved a height of 15.56 meters in the standing high jump, which would have broken the world record, but unfortunately, the equipment was incomplete, resulting in a loss of 8 millimeters, which is a great pity. On the same day, at a meeting in Osaka of the Japan Intercollegiate Athletic Federation's OB alumni living in the Kansai region, Nanbu Chuhei, a graduate of Waseda University, achieved a distance of 7.67 meters in the long jump, also setting a new Japanese record.

Shocking Shanghai's Soccer Scene: The Emergence of the Tunghwa Football Team

Initiator Prefers Anonymity, Dai Linzao Confirmed as Manager

Strength Comparable to the Previous Lok Wah Team

Formal Establishment Planned for September/October

Since the separation of Lok Wah and Chinan, Shanghai's famous soccer players have dispersed and pursued their own paths, worrying many fans who have been waiting for Lok Wah to revive or for the emergence of a similarly strong organization. After much discussion and anticipation within Shanghai's soccer community, there is now some concrete news to share with fans.

The Tunghwa Team Rises in Shanghai

Before recounting the details, the reporter must emphasize that this is not a revival or reorganization of Lok Wah, but rather the emergence of another strong organization, named the Tunghwa Football Team. The team's formation is due to the efforts of a highly respected and enthusiastic individual, one of the many soccer fans. Seeing the importance of public sports and international reputation, and especially since soccer is valued by many countries, this person prepared a meeting and invited famous players to form a new organization. However, before its formal establishment, this person does not wish to reveal his name, stating that it would not add to the facts. However, his pure intentions are similar to those of Cheng Yize, who is currently well-known in the sports world. Dai Linzao has been appointed as the team's manager. Dai is the brother of the well-known center forward Dai Linjing and has good connections in the soccer community, so he will certainly be able to fulfill his duties successfully.

Many Famous Players Return

Responding to the call, many famous soccer players, who were previously wandering and without a place to use their skills, have joined the new organization thanks to the preparations and organization by this enthusiastic individual. The team's key members include Zhou Xianyan, Feng Yunyou, Li Ning, Chen Jiaqiu, Chen Pu, Sun Sijing, Dai Linjing, etc., who recently toured Southeast Asia with the Chinese team (there is also talk of Chen Zhenhe joining the team), as well as the newly returned Tu Kaiyuan and veteran players Chen Yutian and Xi Qiaosheng, etc. The team will be formally established when the touring players return to Shanghai. With such talent, the team is sure to be impressive. Readers, please wait and see.

Record of the Kiangnan Track and Field Team's Northern Expedition (Part 1)

| First Battle: Against the Central Government in Beijing |

Nanjing Dispatch: After arriving in Beijing, the Kiangnan Track and Field Team, in order to make training more interesting, specially invited track and field athletes from National Central University to compete against them.

Kiangnan Not Disappointed: National Central University is China's highest institution of learning, and its Department of Physical Education occupies a particularly important position. Therefore, it has a unique perspective on promoting sports. Even though it was the summer vacation and the athletes had dispersed to their homes, the university resolutely agreed to compete against Kiangnan, with the intention of not disappointing Kiangnan. Indeed, in the results of the competition, Central University won several events.

Acclimatization Reduced Performance: Several strong athletes on the Kiangnan side were unable to participate due to acclimatization and physical discomfort. Others勉强 (miǎnqiǎng - reluctantly/barely) participated in training, but their results were below par, such as Zeng Rongzhong, Chen Xingpei, and Shu Zhaoxian. Furthermore, the long journey during the summer vacation also affected the performance of the other athletes.

Zeng Rongzhong Suffers from Diarrhea: Zeng Rongzhong, the team's 400-meter specialist, suffered from diarrhea after arriving in Nanjing, possibly due to acclimatization. After being treated by Dr. Zhao Shifa, a famous doctor in the capital, it was said to be enteritis, but not very severe and should recover after a few days of treatment.

National Record in Javelin: In all the events, only Wang Jihwai's javelin throw of 47.65 meters broke Wen Dingxin's national record (45.90 meters), which was no small feat.

Wang Fuchen Shows His Skill: At the same time, Wang Fuchen, a coach at the Central Military Academy, also participated in the demonstration, with a javelin throw of 49.10 meters, proving that he is an outstanding javelin thrower. Unfortunately, he has lost his amateur status; otherwise, he would have a great chance of winning the javelin championship at the Double Tenth National Games. The results of each event were already published in yesterday's newspaper and will not be repeated here.

Central University Hosts a Banquet: After the competition, Wu Demao, a lecturer at Central University, representing the Department of Physical Education, invited the entire Kiangnan team to a banquet at the Central Hotel. The teams treated each other courteously and respectfully, and exchanged team flags, ending the evening in good spirits.

Wang Chia-chen Discusses Diplomacy

Long Familiar With Materials on Recovering Concessions

Negotiations With Russia Still Addressing Management of the Chinese Eastern Railway

Vice Minister of Foreign Affairs Wang Chia-chen came to Shanghai on official business the other day. Yesterday, a reporter from the New Sound News Agency interviewed him at his private residence in the French Concession, asking about the recent diplomatic situation as follows:

Recovering Concessions: According to Wang's answer to the reporter's question, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has long been familiar with the materials on recovering concessions in various places and does not need to collect or investigate them. Although the Ministry has appointed Vice Minister Li Chin-lun, Director of the European and American Department Xu Mo, and others as members of the committee, it is only for studying the nature of the concessions. Reports that they have gone to various places for investigation are not true. In the future, negotiations will begin with the Gulangyu, Wuhu, and Yantai (reports say Suzhou, but it should be Yantai) public concessions. The nature of the Wuhu and Yantai concessions is different from that of the Shanghai and Gulangyu public concessions. Shanghai is the largest public concession, while these two public concessions only have management committees and police, without an administrative organization. These two cannot be considered public concessions.

Sino-French Exploration: Regarding the incident of French members of the Sino-French Scientific Exploration Team assaulting Chinese members, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has sent a telegram requesting a formal report before determining the next steps. Rumors that the government has sent a telegram ordering them to stop are unknown to me.

Sino-Russian Negotiations: The Russian side strongly agrees in principle to the redemption of the Chinese Eastern Railway, but this matter cannot be resolved quickly. Currently, the discussions are about the management of the railway, and there is not much progress.

Mi Shuangzhen Case: The case of the Japanese in Liaoyang pouring kerosene and cold water on the Hui Muslim Mi Shuangzhen, resulting in his death, is still being handled at the local level and has not been transferred to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. The Ministry has only seen reports about this case and does not have clear details. Recently, the Ministry has sent a telegram to Shenyang to inquire about everything.

Unified Weights and Measures Implemented in This City Starting Tomorrow

Grand Inspection to Begin on July 11th

Inspectors Have Certificates and Will Not Charge Fees The weights and measures inspection in this city will be unified starting tomorrow and a grand inspection will be implemented starting July 11th. The types of businesses to be inspected, as well as the regulations and procedures, are detailed below:

Implementing the Inspection: The Social Affairs Bureau, following instructions from the Ministry of Industry, will announce the unification of weights and measures starting tomorrow. The use of old weights and measures will be prohibited from this date. However, due to the particularly chaotic situation in the city's vegetable markets, the unification will be implemented in advance on June 1st. A grand inspection will be conducted starting July 11th in conjunction with the public security authorities. The first phase will be in the Hunan District, the second phase will be in the Zhabei District, the third phase will be in the Concession District, and the fourth phase will be in the four rural districts. Six inspectors will be dispatched each day, divided into four groups, to inspect approximately 100 businesses per day, using the roads as units.

Inspection Regulations: The regulations for the implementation of weights and measures inspection are as follows: (Article 1) All weights and measures used by government agencies and for commercial purposes should be inspected in accordance with these regulations. (Article 2) Weights and measures inspections should be carried out once a year on a regular basis, but temporary inspections may be carried out when necessary. (Article 3) The area and date of the inspection should be announced in advance by the local weights and measures inspection office or branch in conjunction with the public security authority. (Article 4) Inspectors, accompanied by police officers, should visit the various agencies and households within each area during daily service hours to inspect weights and measures. (Article 5) All agencies and households newly established or relocated within the inspected area should, in accordance with the notice of the public security authority, submit the weights and measures they use for supplementary inspection or proof of verification. (Article 6) Inspectors should carry a certificate proving that they have been dispatched for inspection. The certificate must be affixed with a two-and-a-half-inch photograph of the inspector. (Article 7) No fees will be charged for the inspection of weights and measures. (Article 8) Weights and measures that pass inspection should be stamped with an inspection mark or given a certificate. (Article 9) Weights and measures that have been inspected should be registered in detail by the local inspection office or branch. (Article 10) Each local weights and measures inspection office or branch should report the details and results of each inspection to the National Bureau of Weights and Measures. (Article 11) Factories, shops, and households within the inspected area must not use weights and measures that have not been inspected, stamped, or given a certificate. (Article 12) If weights and measures that have been inspected and stamped or given a certificate are found to be inconsistent, the local weights and measures inspection office or branch may conduct a temporary inspection in conjunction with the public security authority. (Article 13) Anyone who forges an inspection office's stamp or certificate, or uses such a stamp or certificate fraudulently, will be fined between ten and one hundred yuan and punished in accordance with the relevant articles of the Criminal Code. (Article 14) Anyone who impersonates an inspector should be sent to court for legal punishment. (Article 15) If an inspector engages in illegal or fraudulent activities, he should be dismissed and sent to court for legal punishment. (Article 16) Anyone who violates the provisions of Article 11 will be fined five yuan or more. (Article 17) The date of implementation of these regulations will be determined by a separate order of the Ministry.

Industries to be Inspected: The following 43 industries are designated by the inspection office for initial inspection in the 20th year of the Republic for the use of new weights and measures in industry and commerce: cloth industry, tofu industry, silk industry, fresh fish industry, garment industry, cattle leather goods industry, Western-style clothing industry, leather industry, weaving industry, wool skin and bone industry, knitting industry, fur industry, shoe and hat industry, pewter industry, rice industry, woodworking industry, grain industry, rosewood industry, flour industry, coal and firewood industry, miscellaneous fruit and canned food industry, plank industry, local goods and fruit industry, brick and ash industry, pig, sheep, chicken, and duck industry, pawnshop industry, soy sauce and wine industry, oil and hemp industry, tea and pastry industry, secondhand goods industry, cooked food industry, cotton batting industry, fresh meat industry, yarn industry, cooked meat and game industry, paint industry, pickled and salted fish industry, water pipe industry, northern and southern goods industry, medicinal materials industry, tea industry, ginseng and bird's nest industry, hardware industry, etc. Other industries and places will be inspected after the commercial inspection is completed.

Types of Instruments: There are many types of weights and measures. The following is a breakdown: (1) Types of length measures: ruler, carpenter's square, tape measure, chain measure, etc. (2) Types of volume measures: hu, dou, sheng, he, etc. (3) Types of weight measures: hook scales, small scales, platform scales, balance scales, named scales, etc. There are also scientific instruments, gas meters, water meters, electricity meters, surveying instruments, etc., which are all special types of weights and measures.

Director Zhou Speaks: Zhou Zanming, director of the Weights and Measures Inspection Office, told a reporter from the New Sound News Agency yesterday that the weights and measures used in our country have always been freely manufactured by the people, without any standards, leading to the chaotic situation of today. Leaving aside the past, there are probably no fewer than hundreds of types still circulating among the people. The difference in the capacity of each instrument not only varies with the locality and business, but also varies greatly even within the same locality or the same business, and even within the same business in the same locality. In addition, there are also differences in the length, size, weight, etc. of instruments of the same type. The instruments that will be destroyed in this inspection are only those weights and measures that are beyond repair, such as the small instruments used by vegetable vendors. According to Article 47 of the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the Weights and Measures Act, those that are deemed irreparable during inspection should be destroyed. As for weights and measures that are found to be inconsistent during the upcoming grand inspection, they will be stamped as unqualified or instructed to be modified. However, those that are beyond repair must still be destroyed.

Cracking Down on Japanese Fishing Vessels

Strictly Prohibiting Encroachment on Territorial Waters

To Be Implemented Starting Tomorrow

Japanese fishing vessels entering our country's territorial waters to fish freely, and even driving away our fishing vessels, treating us as guests in our own home, has been repeatedly protested by various central government departments to the Japanese side. Subsequently, the Ministries of Foreign Affairs, Finance, Industry, and the Navy held a meeting and clearly defined the boundaries of territorial waters, stipulating that Japanese fishing vessels may not enter within twelve nautical miles of our country's sea surface. It has now been decided that this restriction on territorial waters will be implemented starting July 1st. The various ministries have ordered the customs offices and instructed the Naval Headquarters to pass the order to patrol boats and warships. Starting July 1st, if Japanese fishing vessels again encroach within the defined twelve nautical miles to fish, it will be considered a violation of our territorial waters and fishing rights. The warships are authorized to expel them. If they refuse to comply, they may be detained and handed over to the Japanese authorities for punishment.

Yesterday's Conflict Between Wusong Anti-Smuggling Camp and Public Security Bureau Police

Serious Situation… Shops Panicked

Army Suppression… Finally Calmed

Yesterday afternoon at approximately 3:00 PM, a conflict occurred between soldiers from the First Brigade of the Anti-Smuggling Corps, which belongs to Jiangsu Province and is stationed on the Wusong Outer Bund, and police officers from the First Precinct of the Seventh District Public Security Bureau due to a minor misunderstanding. The situation became serious, and nearby shops panicked and closed their doors. Upon receiving the news, Battalion Commander Xiong of the Second Battalion of the 27th Regiment, Fifth Division stationed in Wusong, quickly dispatched troops to suppress the conflict, and it was eventually calmed. The details are recorded below:

Urination Incident: The day before yesterday (the 28th), at approximately 5:30 AM, Huang Guiqing, a soldier from the First Patrol Boat, First Brigade of the Anti-Smuggling Corps, dressed in plain clothes, was urinating on a vacant lot at the intersection of Doushi Road and Yu Tong Road in Wusong. Officer Gao Yunian of the First Precinct of the Seventh District noticed this and immediately intervened. Soldier Huang then fled back to the patrol boat moored on the Pujiang River off the Outer Bund. Officer Gao pursued him onto the boat to arrest him, and a conflict ensued. It escalated into violence, and Gao was injured. He returned to the precinct to report the incident. Afterward, the Anti-Smuggling Corps apologized to the First Precinct, and the matter was settled.

Police Officer Assaulted: Unexpectedly, yesterday (the 29th) at 11:00 AM, Zhang Falin, a soldier from the Fourth Patrol Boat of the Anti-Smuggling Corps, was walking from south to north when he passed the Yunzaobang Bridge. For unknown reasons, he suddenly clashed with a police officer from the First Precinct, resulting in Zhang sustaining serious injuries. He returned to report this to the other soldiers, who were enraged upon hearing the news. At approximately 3:00 PM, Yu, the helmsman of the First Patrol Boat, gathered more than ten people and marched to the intersection of Yu Tong Road, dragging two patrol officers, Liu Hongji and Ma Zhilin, from their posts at Songyu Road to the corps headquarters, eventually causing them injuries.

Shops Panicked: When Liu and others were injured, they immediately blew their whistles frantically. Armed police officers from the precinct's patrol team, upon hearing the alarm, rushed to the Anti-Smuggling Corps headquarters as if facing a major enemy. At that time, a gunshot was heard, and nearby shops immediately panicked and closed their doors. The situation was extremely serious. Battalion Commander Xiong Kexi of the Second Battalion of the 27th Regiment, Fifth Division of the Army stationed in Wusong, upon receiving the news, considering it concerned local security, immediately led more than twenty soldiers armed with live ammunition to suppress the situation. The incident was eventually calmed.

Mediation Unsuccessful: An investigation revealed that Zhang Maocai, a bugler in the Anti-Smuggling Corps, was injured, and a bullet hole was found in the ceiling downstairs in the corps headquarters, but the floorboard was not penetrated. The injured soldiers and police officers were all sent to Wusong Haibin Public Hospital for treatment. That evening at 8:00 PM, Battalion Commander Xiong convened a meeting with Zhao Zezhou, the District Chief of the Seventh District Public Security Bureau, Zhang Jiguang, the Chief of the First Precinct of the Seventh District, and Li Huchen, the Captain of the Anti-Smuggling Corps, to discuss mediation. The superiors of both sides have reported the matter to their superiors and requested instructions.

Shanghai Municipal Council's Measures for Collecting Municipal General Tax

Changing to Public Notice Method

Equal Treatment for Chinese and Foreigners

The Shanghai Municipal Council's method for collecting municipal general taxes on foreign-style houses within the Settlement has been to issue notices 14 days in advance, then send tax collectors to collect the taxes. A month ago, the Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers' Association repeatedly urged the Municipal Council to provide equal treatment for Chinese and foreigners, and to issue notices 14 days in advance for Chinese-style houses as well so that taxpayers could prepare accordingly. It is now reported that the Municipal Council, to show equal treatment for Chinese and foreigners, has cancelled the practice of issuing advance notices for foreign-style houses and has adopted a public notice method, publishing notices in both Chinese and foreign newspapers. The following is the Public Notice No. 4109 regarding the collection of the autumn general tax: Public Notice: It is hereby notified that the tax on all types of Chinese and foreign houses for the quarter ending September 30th of this year is due on July 1st and collection will begin on that date. All tax payments should be made to the Council's tax collectors or directly to the Tax Office at 209 Jiangxi Road. This notice is hereby announced. Acting Secretary-General, Mackie.

Landlords Should Obtain Guarantees from Tenants

Notice from the Real Estate Association

The Shanghai Real Estate Association sent a circular to its member real estate companies yesterday, stating: "We are writing to inform you that we have received a letter from the Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers' Association stating that Article 5 of the Regulations for the Punishment of Kidnappers stipulates that landlords should obtain guarantees from tenants. To prevent kidnapping, in addition to writing to the Municipal Council for assistance in implementing this regulation, we are writing to your association to inform all members to comply accordingly." It is understood that landlords obtaining guarantees from tenants has already been implemented under the jurisdiction of the Shanghai Municipal Government, but it is still rare in the Special District. Previously, it was possible to choose freely, and as long as the rent was paid, there were no major difficulties. Now, legislators, in order to prevent kidnapping and eliminate it completely, have specially formulated the Regulations for the Punishment of Kidnappers, and Article 5 specifically stipulates that landlords must obtain guarantees from tenants. This regulation was promulgated and implemented by the National Government long ago. Fortunately, in the case of the Youtong Company's houses on Wuding Road, the landlord had obtained guarantees from the tenants, otherwise it would not have been easy to overturn the confiscation. In accordance with the aforementioned letter, we are writing to inform you, hoping that you will investigate and handle this matter promptly, in order to comply with the law and prevent kidnapping. If tenants object and it is difficult to implement, the Chinese Ratepayers' Association has already written to the authorities in the Special District requesting assistance. You can report the matter directly to the police station.

Ziqiang Warship Conducted Trial Run and Gunnery Test Again Yesterday

Awaiting Reorganization

After a trial run in the Longhua area, the Ziqiang warship, under the command of Captain Qiu Shizhong, naval ordnance supervisor Zheng Zichi, shipyard director Yu Jianfu, and various supervisors, set sail from 6:00 AM yesterday morning and headed to the outer Wusong estuary for gunnery and navigation tests. A total of twelve 5.1-inch cannons at the bow and stern of the ship fired twice each, with a range of 10,000 yards. The recoil was about 9 inches. The sound was thunderous. Two shells hit the target below, two shells were slightly ahead, and one was slightly behind, with a difference of about 20 yards. After the test, the 3-inch cannons and the German 20mm Oerlikon anti-aircraft guns were also tested. The results were very satisfactory. The Oerlikon anti-aircraft gun shells were fired in a chain, and their agility and stability were particularly outstanding. The tests ended at 11:00 AM, and then the maximum speed test began, reaching 19 knots per hour, which is one knot faster than the Datong warship. The turning, reversing, and manpower navigation were also more agile and better than the Datong. The tests were completed at 5:00 PM, and the ship returned to Gaochangmiao at 7:00 PM to await reorganization.

Employees of the National Products Department Store to Petition Today Regarding the Case

Regarding the Municipal Council's Order to Close the National Products Department Store Case: After repeated discussions by the Negotiating Committee of the Chinese Directors of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, a resolution has been reached. For the sake of their livelihoods, all employees will go to the Municipal Government, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Chinese Ratepayers' Association, and the Citizens' General Association today to petition. The various situations yesterday are recorded as follows:

Emergency General Meeting: All employees of the National Products Department Store convened an emergency general meeting at 10:00 AM yesterday. Li Weicheng was elected temporary chairman. Chen Weixin and Liu Musu reported on the negotiation process. The following resolutions were passed: (1) It was decided that tomorrow (the 30th) at 10:00 AM, all 600 employees would carry the negotiation terms and depart to petition the Municipal Government, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Chinese Ratepayers' Association, and the Citizens' United Association. (2) It was decided that this afternoon, six representatives would be selected to ask Mr. Li Zhengwu for help to maintain the employees' situation. It was also heard that the association would certify that the negotiation regarding the Department Store's illegal closure and the assault on staff by the Municipal Council has not been resolved after more than 20 days, and the union will automatically respond.

Petition: The petition from all employees of the National Products Department Store to the Municipal Government, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and the Chinese Ratepayers' Association is as follows: We, the assembled employees, respectfully petition, requesting that you promptly engage in serious negotiations with the Municipal Council to resolve this outstanding case, uphold national rights, protect national products, and maintain the employees' livelihoods. We respectfully request your attention to this matter. The cause of the Department Store's illegal closure by the Municipal Council has been reported by the Negotiating Committee of the Department Store to the Central Government and your office, requesting serious negotiations and proposing seven conditions for resolving the case. The employees have been quietly waiting for a resolution and dare not rashly interfere. However, we believe that the closure of the Department Store has lasted for more than 20 days, which is not a short time, and the date of resolution is still far away and hopeless. The employees have suffered since the incident. Not only can the sweat and labor wages not be paid by the Department Store, but even daily meals can no longer be provided by the Department Store. If this case is further delayed, the lives of hundreds of employees and the livelihoods of thousands of family members can only perish together. This is a real cause for midnight anxiety, and we cannot help but speak out. The Municipal Council previously asked the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to mediate. In its verbal and written reports at the meeting, it admitted the mistake of closing the Department Store, which undoubtedly bears legal responsibility. Furthermore, according to the seven conditions proposed by the Department Store to the Municipal Council, the claims are based on reason and do not make excessive demands. If the Municipal Council is truly determined to repent, it should accept the conditions as soon as possible and restore the Department Store's business. However, after admitting the mistake, it has made no other representation. How can such a major case be dealt with by simply glossing over it with the word "mistake"? Its intention is to maintain its imperialistic stance, adhere to its power, and oppress the weak. There is no so-called justice, let alone law. The admission of error in the report to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce was merely to ease the anti-imperialist movement of our people and cool down our anti-imperialist enthusiasm, so that after a long delay, the Department Store would disappear without a trace, and the case could be left unresolved like various past cases. Its plan can be said to be very clever, and its intention can be said to be very vicious. In order to protect the Department Store's life and the livelihoods of thousands of employees, in addition to establishing the National Products Department Store Employees' United Association as the Department Store's support, we specially present our grievances. All employees respectfully petition, requesting that your office grant us an audience, listen to our opinions, promptly engage in serious negotiations with the Municipal Council, and resolve the matter as soon as possible, so that national rights can be upheld, national products can be developed, and the Department Store's life and the employees' lives can be extended.

Qu Case to Be Heard This Morning

The "Shanghai Evening Post" reported that the Qu case involving three American soldiers will be heard in military court tomorrow morning (the 30th). The trial will be open to the public and presided over by Lieutenant Colonel Buck. Major Osherthore and six others will serve as judges. Captain Dayle will be the prosecutor. Corporal Monn is accused of four counts of misconduct and disrupting public order. Orderly Daniel is accused of three counts of violating discipline, illegally assaulting people, and being drunk. Orderly Ginass is also accused of illegally assaulting people. The trial is scheduled to begin at 9:00 AM. Reporters and the public are welcome to attend. Orderly Dominic was also detained by the American authorities at the time, but was released after it was determined that he had not been involved.

Tomorrow and the day after (July 1st), Chinese and foreign banks on the Bund will close for two days as usual for the semi-annual accounting period. They will reopen on the 3rd (Friday) as usual. It is reported that during the closure period, bank staff will continue to work, but business with the public will be temporarily suspended, so the situation is very different from the usual closure.
